\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cast\_op\_type}{cast\_op\_type}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T $>$ \\
using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_abd8bac29f0de8fe374d7567dfb8bee8d}{pybind11\+::detail\+::cast\+\_\+op\+\_\+type}} = typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aef2d4be22c22106ff1a07aeb9394fb60}{conditional\+\_\+t}}$<$std\+::is\+\_\+pointer$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a6c207068b00c8f12378fe4e8f02eaa73}{remove\+\_\+reference\+\_\+t}}$<$T$>$ $>$\+::value, typename std\+::add\+\_\+pointer$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aa37a5957cbb8ad416e9c0a3a9e0c365e}{intrinsic\+\_\+t}}$<$T$>$ $>$\+::\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a2e27b6b0496dbceae6708f0526822bba}{type}}, typename std\+::add\+\_\+lvalue\+\_\+reference$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aa37a5957cbb8ad416e9c0a3a9e0c365e}{intrinsic\+\_\+t}}$<$T$>$ $>$\+::\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a2e27b6b0496dbceae6708f0526822bba}{type}}$>$}

Determine suitable casting operator for pointer-\/or-\/lvalue-\/casting type casters. The type caster needs to provide {\ttfamily operator T$\ast$()} and {\ttfamily operator T\&()} operators.

If the type supports moving the value away via an {\ttfamily operator T\&\&() \&\&} method, it should use {\ttfamily movable\+\_\+cast\+\_\+op\+\_\+type} instead. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aef2d4be22c22106ff1a07aeb9394fb60}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aef2d4be22c22106ff1a07aeb9394fb60}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a5fcc977e92be71760b66c8c671e79634}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a5fcc977e92be71760b66c8c671e79634}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!forwarded\_type@{forwarded\_type}}
\index{forwarded\_type@{forwarded\_type}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{forwarded\_type}{forwarded\_type}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T , typename U $>$ \\
using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a5fcc977e92be71760b66c8c671e79634}{pybind11\+::detail\+::forwarded\+\_\+type}} = typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aef2d4be22c22106ff1a07aeb9394fb60}{conditional\+\_\+t}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+lvalue\+\_\+reference$<$T$>$\+::value, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a6c207068b00c8f12378fe4e8f02eaa73}{remove\+\_\+reference\+\_\+t}}$<$U$>$ \&, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a6c207068b00c8f12378fe4e8f02eaa73}{remove\+\_\+reference\+\_\+t}}$<$U$>$ \&\&$>$}

Extracts an const lvalue reference or rvalue reference for U based on the type of T (e.\+g. for forwarding a container element). Typically used indirect via \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a5fcc977e92be71760b66c8c671e79634}{forwarded\+\_\+type()}}, below. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aa37a5957cbb8ad416e9c0a3a9e0c365e}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aa37a5957cbb8ad416e9c0a3a9e0c365e}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{movable\_cast\_op\_type}{movable\_cast\_op\_type}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T $>$ \\
using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a3e4f52c827f0391c3ca8166590c559c9}{pybind11\+::detail\+::movable\+\_\+cast\+\_\+op\+\_\+type}} = typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aef2d4be22c22106ff1a07aeb9394fb60}{conditional\+\_\+t}}$<$std\+::is\+\_\+pointer$<$typename std\+::remove\+\_\+reference$<$T$>$\+::\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a2e27b6b0496dbceae6708f0526822bba}{type}}$>$\+::value, typename std\+::add\+\_\+pointer$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aa37a5957cbb8ad416e9c0a3a9e0c365e}{intrinsic\+\_\+t}}$<$T$>$ $>$\+::\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a2e27b6b0496dbceae6708f0526822bba}{type}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aef2d4be22c22106ff1a07aeb9394fb60}{conditional\+\_\+t}}$<$std\+::is\+\_\+rvalue\+\_\+reference$<$T$>$\+::value, typename std\+::add\+\_\+rvalue\+\_\+reference$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aa37a5957cbb8ad416e9c0a3a9e0c365e}{intrinsic\+\_\+t}}$<$T$>$ $>$\+::\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a2e27b6b0496dbceae6708f0526822bba}{type}}, typename std\+::add\+\_\+lvalue\+\_\+reference$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aa37a5957cbb8ad416e9c0a3a9e0c365e}{intrinsic\+\_\+t}}$<$T$>$ $>$\+::\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a2e27b6b0496dbceae6708f0526822bba}{type}}$>$ $>$}

Determine suitable casting operator for a type caster with a movable value. Such a type caster needs to provide {\ttfamily operator T$\ast$()}, {\ttfamily operator T\&()}, and {\ttfamily operator T\&\&() \&\&}. The latter will be called in appropriate contexts where the value can be moved rather than copied.

These operator are automatically provided when using the PYBIND11\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+CASTER macro. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_ab96eb0dc6544902fbae045953bd5075f}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_ab96eb0dc6544902fbae045953bd5075f}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!move\_is\_plain\_type@{move\_is\_plain\_type}}
\index{move\_is\_plain\_type@{move\_is\_plain\_type}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{move\_is\_plain\_type}{move\_is\_plain\_type}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a467e32cfb22b4efc77c489b9d4663164}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a467e32cfb22b4efc77c489b9d4663164}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_\_attribute\_\_()}{\_\_attribute\_\_()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily pybind11\+::detail\+::\+\_\+\+\_\+attribute\+\_\+\+\_\+ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{(noinline)}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) \&\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aeb4a9b9dcaab655056540151fa1da0e6}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aeb4a9b9dcaab655056540151fa1da0e6}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!\_\_attribute\_\_@{\_\_attribute\_\_}}
\index{\_\_attribute\_\_@{\_\_attribute\_\_}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_\_attribute\_\_()}{\_\_attribute\_\_()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily pybind11\+::detail\+::\+\_\+\+\_\+attribute\+\_\+\+\_\+ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{(noinline)}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Gets a single \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11}{pybind11}} type info for a python type. Returns nullptr if neither the type nor any ancestors are pybind11-\/registered. Throws an exception if there are multiple bases--use {\ttfamily all\+\_\+type\+\_\+info} instead if you want to support multiple bases.

Extracts C++ value and holder pointer references from an instance (which may contain multiple values/holders for python-\/side multiple inheritance) that match the given type. Throws an error if the given type (or Value\+Type, if omitted) is not a \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11}{pybind11}} base of the given instance. If {\ttfamily find\+\_\+type} is omitted (or explicitly specified as nullptr) the first value/holder are returned, regardless of type (and the resulting .type will be nullptr).

The returned object should be short-\/lived\+: in particular, it must not outlive the called-\/upon instance. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_af668c2d777879646e5f3e905b6dc4de2}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_af668c2d777879646e5f3e905b6dc4de2}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!\_\_self@{\_\_self}}
\index{\_\_self@{\_\_self}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_\_self()}{\_\_self()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1self__t}{self\+\_\+t}} pybind11\+::detail\+::\+\_\+\+\_\+self (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Don\textquotesingle{}t warn about an unused variable. 

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_ac475f67e781e0c607a75072acb5d11d2}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_ac475f67e781e0c607a75072acb5d11d2}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1op__}{op\+\_\+}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a60eaefc77d8e336f21b31425d79e0111a2a6aef482b2afa4b6f2c0dfce5735016}{op\+\_\+abs}} , \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aab1046200267d81fe97a73f1c99bca53acf71f03d926dc4d086b63e4aeefb76c1}{op\+\_\+u}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1self__t}{self\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1undefined__t}{undefined\+\_\+t}}$>$ pybind11\+::detail\+::abs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1self__t}{self\+\_\+t}} \&}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_af62c3b270c006fce8eb96756ca0c3979}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_af62c3b270c006fce8eb96756ca0c3979}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{add\_patient()}{add\_patient()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void pybind11\+::detail\+::add\+\_\+patient (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Py\+Object $\ast$}]{nurse,  }\item[{Py\+Object $\ast$}]{patient }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a369ebb69a9a6490d8814cd466acee5a4}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a369ebb69a9a6490d8814cd466acee5a4}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!all\_type\_info@{all\_type\_info}}
\index{all\_type\_info@{all\_type\_info}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{all\_type\_info()}{all\_type\_info()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const std\+::vector$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1type__info}{detail\+::type\+\_\+info}} $\ast$$>$\& pybind11\+::detail\+::all\+\_\+type\+\_\+info (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Py\+Type\+Object $\ast$}]{type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Extracts vector of \mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1type__info}{type\+\_\+info}} pointers of pybind-\/registered roots of the given Python type. Will be just 1 pybind type for the Python type of a pybind-\/registered class, or for any Python-\/side derived class that uses single inheritance. Will contain as many types as required for a Python class that uses multiple inheritance to inherit (directly or indirectly) from multiple pybind-\/registered classes. Will be empty if neither the type nor any base classes are pybind-\/registered.

The value is cached for the lifetime of the Python type. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a7920862bbd224b2e0a9a2b02325b4b39}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a7920862bbd224b2e0a9a2b02325b4b39}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{all\_type\_info\_get\_cache()}{all\_type\_info\_get\_cache()}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily constexpr \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11_a74292751b6fc8fe14d7c6772ae2fd0fc}{size\+\_\+t}} pybind11\+::detail\+::instance\+\_\+simple\+\_\+holder\+\_\+in\+\_\+ptrs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [constexpr]}}

The space to allocate for simple layout instance holders (see below) in multiple of the size of a pointer (e.\+g. 2 means 16 bytes on 64-\/bit architectures). The default is the minimum required to holder either a std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr or std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr (which is almost always sizeof(std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr$<$\+T$>$)). \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a20fe1c2f5fbb219cb211956780afee53}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a20fe1c2f5fbb219cb211956780afee53}}

This metaclass is assigned by default to all \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11}{pybind11}} types and is required in order for static properties to function correctly. Users may override this using {\ttfamily py\+::metaclass}. Return value\+: New reference. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a6295a3814da747beecb99da3095ddb00}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a6295a3814da747beecb99da3095ddb00}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!make\_new\_instance@{make\_new\_instance}}
\index{make\_new\_instance@{make\_new\_instance}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{make\_new\_instance()}{make\_new\_instance()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Py\+Object $\ast$ pybind11\+::detail\+::make\+\_\+new\+\_\+instance (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Py\+Type\+Object $\ast$}]{type,  }\item[{bool}]{allocate\+\_\+value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Instance creation function for all \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11}{pybind11}} types. It only allocates space for the C++ object (or multiple objects, for Python-\/side inheritance from multiple \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11}{pybind11}} types), but doesn\textquotesingle{}t call the constructor -- an {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+init\+\_\+\+\_\+} function must do that. If allocating value, the instance is registered; otherwise register\+\_\+instance will need to be called once the value has been assigned. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a0fe1a62ca38562fd83993b3abf9c49fd}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a0fe1a62ca38562fd83993b3abf9c49fd}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!make\_new\_python\_type@{make\_new\_python\_type}}
\index{make\_new\_python\_type@{make\_new\_python\_type}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{make\_new\_python\_type()}{make\_new\_python\_type()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Py\+Object$\ast$ pybind11\+::detail\+::make\+\_\+new\+\_\+python\+\_\+type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1type__record}{type\+\_\+record}} \&}]{rec }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Create a brand new Python type according to the {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1type__record}{type\+\_\+record}}} specification. Return value\+: New reference. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a4aad17fe209f5c6187910481e33654f1}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a4aad17fe209f5c6187910481e33654f1}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{make\_object\_base\_type()}{make\_object\_base\_type()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Py\+Object $\ast$ pybind11\+::detail\+::make\+\_\+object\+\_\+base\+\_\+type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Py\+Type\+Object $\ast$}]{metaclass }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Py\+Type\+Object $\ast$ pybind11\+::detail\+::make\+\_\+static\+\_\+property\+\_\+type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

A {\ttfamily static\+\_\+property} is the same as a {\ttfamily property} but the {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+get\+\_\+\+\_\+()} and {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+set\+\_\+\+\_\+()} methods are modified to always use the object type instead of a concrete instance. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_af890f322200bd699e7aaa8da55a97428}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_af890f322200bd699e7aaa8da55a97428}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!pybind11\_meta\_setattro@{pybind11\_meta\_setattro}}
\index{pybind11\_meta\_setattro@{pybind11\_meta\_setattro}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pybind11\_meta\_setattro()}{pybind11\_meta\_setattro()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int pybind11\+::detail\+::pybind11\+\_\+meta\+\_\+setattro (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Py\+Object $\ast$}]{obj,  }\item[{Py\+Object $\ast$}]{name,  }\item[{Py\+Object $\ast$}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Types with static properties need to handle {\ttfamily Type.\+static\+\_\+prop = x} in a specific way. By default, Python replaces the {\ttfamily static\+\_\+property} itself, but for wrapped C++ types we need to call {\ttfamily static\+\_\+property.\+\_\+\+\_\+set\+\_\+\+\_\+()} in order to propagate the new value to the underlying C++ data structure. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a06542d285d3812cea1e7b26008360912}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a06542d285d3812cea1e7b26008360912}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!pybind11\_object\_dealloc@{pybind11\_object\_dealloc}}
\index{pybind11\_object\_dealloc@{pybind11\_object\_dealloc}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pybind11\_object\_dealloc()}{pybind11\_object\_dealloc()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void pybind11\+::detail\+::pybind11\+\_\+object\+\_\+dealloc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Py\+Object $\ast$}]{self }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Instance destructor function for all \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11}{pybind11}} types. It calls {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1type__info_ac2d391b653920f0b0506001042dffed2}{type\+\_\+info.\+dealloc}}} to destroy the C++ object itself, while the rest is Python bookkeeping. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a21c40030f5a35e6135753ba25dc5fbe4}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a21c40030f5a35e6135753ba25dc5fbe4}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!pybind11\_object\_init@{pybind11\_object\_init}}
\index{pybind11\_object\_init@{pybind11\_object\_init}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pybind11\_object\_init()}{pybind11\_object\_init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int pybind11\+::detail\+::pybind11\+\_\+object\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Py\+Object $\ast$}]{self,  }\item[{Py\+Object $\ast$}]{,  }\item[{Py\+Object $\ast$}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

An {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+init\+\_\+\+\_\+} function constructs the C++ object. Users should provide at least one of these using {\ttfamily py\+::init} or directly with {\ttfamily .def(\+\_\+\+\_\+init\+\_\+\+\_\+, ...)}. Otherwise, the following default function will be used which simply throws an exception. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_acdfc8125a018f1d1b47a8dec119cf17d}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_acdfc8125a018f1d1b47a8dec119cf17d}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!pybind11\_object\_new@{pybind11\_object\_new}}
\index{pybind11\_object\_new@{pybind11\_object\_new}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pybind11\_object\_new()}{pybind11\_object\_new()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Py\+Object$\ast$ pybind11\+::detail\+::pybind11\+\_\+object\+\_\+new (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Py\+Type\+Object $\ast$}]{type,  }\item[{Py\+Object $\ast$}]{,  }\item[{Py\+Object $\ast$}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Instance creation function for all \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepybind11}{pybind11}} types. It only allocates space for the C++ object, but doesn\textquotesingle{}t call the constructor -- an {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+init\+\_\+\+\_\+} function must do that. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a25d421a8dfae2015037edd61590a7374}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a25d421a8dfae2015037edd61590a7374}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aad403360b3f798558436b37ea0272492}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aad403360b3f798558436b37ea0272492}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!set\_operator\_new@{set\_operator\_new}}
\index{set\_operator\_new@{set\_operator\_new}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_operator\_new()}{set\_operator\_new()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename $>$ \\
void pybind11\+::detail\+::set\+\_\+operator\+\_\+new (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{... }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aac9fbec63a815cf6e602a9c235ca7533}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_aac9fbec63a815cf6e602a9c235ca7533}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!set\_operator\_new@{set\_operator\_new}}
\index{set\_operator\_new@{set\_operator\_new}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{set\_operator\_new()}{set\_operator\_new()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T , typename  = void\+\_\+t$<$decltype(static\+\_\+cast$<$void $\ast$($\ast$)(size\+\_\+t)$>$(\+T\+::operator new))$>$$>$ \\
void pybind11\+::detail\+::set\+\_\+operator\+\_\+new (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1type__record}{type\+\_\+record}} $\ast$}]{r }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the pointer to operator new if it exists. The cast is needed because it can be overloaded. 

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a67d4396e43eb0554341545e975e11deb}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a67d4396e43eb0554341545e975e11deb}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!traverse\_offset\_bases@{traverse\_offset\_bases}}
\index{traverse\_offset\_bases@{traverse\_offset\_bases}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{traverse\_offset\_bases()}{traverse\_offset\_bases()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void pybind11\+::detail\+::traverse\+\_\+offset\+\_\+bases (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{valueptr,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1type__info}{detail\+::type\+\_\+info}} $\ast$}]{tinfo,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1instance}{instance}} $\ast$}]{self,  }\item[{bool($\ast$)(void $\ast$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structpybind11_1_1detail_1_1instance}{instance}} $\ast$)}]{f }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

For multiple inheritance types we need to recursively register/deregister base pointers for any base classes with pointers that are difference from the instance value pointer so that we can correctly recognize an offset base class pointer. This calls a function with any offset base ptrs. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a5baa19168451e7acf7a909b8a1b55206}\label{namespacepybind11_1_1detail_a5baa19168451e7acf7a909b8a1b55206}} 
\index{pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}!type\_incref@{type\_incref}}
\index{type\_incref@{type\_incref}!pybind11::detail@{pybind11::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{type\_incref()}{type\_incref()}}
